1b1(mdo): rtsa gar skad du/ ma hA kA ru na pun d+ha ri ka na ma ma hA ya na su tra// bod skad du
1b2(mdo): snying rje chen po yi pad ma dkar po zhes bya ba theg po'i mdo// sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa'
1b3(mdo): thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das ku ka'i grong
1b4(mdo): byer na/ kyang rnams nye bar gnas pa/ shing sa la yi tshal na bzhugs so// de nas
1b5(mdo): bcom ldan 'das yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba'i dus kyi tshe/ tshedang ldan pa kun
1b6(mdo): dka' bo la bka' su lad pa/ kun dka' bo de bzhin gshegs pa do mod kyi rnam kyi thun tham la
1b7(mdo): yongs su mya dngasas 'das/ khyod kyis shing sa la zung gi bar du de bzhin gshegs pa seng ge ltar grogams
1b8(mdo): byas marnam pa'i gzims mal 'chom zhin/ kun dga' bo 'dus byas su btags pa thams cad legs par
2a1(mdo): rgyas kyi bya ba ni byas/ ngas gnas myed pa'i chos zhib/ rab tu zhib/ mchog/ gya nol pa/ zab pa/ mthong bar da/ 'a ba/ 'ong du chud par dga' ba/ btag kyi nus pa/ ma btags
2a2(mdo): pa/ rtog ge ba'i spyod yul ma yin pa/ mkhas pa dang / 'angangs pas rig pa/ bul du mi dad par 'phags pa'i bdud rtsi bsta dang / kun dga' bo ngas chos kyi 'khor lo bla na myed pa/ dge sbyong ngam
2a3(mdo): zas ze 'am/ bdud das/ lha 'am/ rangs pa'am/ gzhan gang gis kyang / chos dang mthun par 'jig rten du ma bskor dang / lan gsum du bzlas te/ rnas pa bcu gnyis su bskor ba ni bskor/ ras
2a4(mdo): chos kyi chechen po ni brdungs/ ngas chos kyi dung chen po ni bus ngas chos kyi rgyal mchad chen po ni bsgreng / ngas chos kyi mar rtse chen po ni bus/ ngas mud pa chen po ribs yang/ ngas stong
2a5(mdo): gsum ni sdang bar byas/ ngas klu chen po ni bcas/ ngas stegs chen po ni btsugs/ ngas zam pa chen po ni btags/ ngas pha rol 'dong pa mang po ni ston// ngas tha rad pa'i lam
2a6(mdo): de yang dag par bstadang / ngas chos kyi mar ched po de phab ngas lha dang kyi rnams ni ris par byas/ ngas 'dul ba rnams ni 'dul / ngas pas kyi rgol ba thams cad ni skrag par byas/
2a7(mdo): dus su stegs kyi gnas thams cad de du yang / sa bdud kyi stobs de / dus 'du kyi grangs rigs par nus/ dus the ge'i sgra ni bsgrags/ ras sangs rgyas ci bye ba ni byas/ ngas kyis nu das pa'i
2a8(mdo): nim par phyung / ngas sngon gyi yi das ni yongs su rdzogs par byas/ ngas chos kyi tshul ni byid kyis brlabs/ ngas nyan thos chen po rnams las byed du ni btsud/ ma 'ongs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi tshul rgyun myi 'chad par/
2a9(mdo): bya ba'i phyir/ ras byang chub sems da' sems dpa' chen po rnams lung ni bstan ba dad te/ kun dga' bo mya ngan las 'das pa ma rtogs par/ phyis bya ba pal myed do// de nas tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' ba
2b1(mdo): bcom ldan 'das kyi gsung rnam pa de lta bu de thos nas/ sdug bsngal zhing yid kyi bde ste/ myi dga' zhing mya ngan chen po'i zug rngu zug par gyu rud nas/ rab tu ngus te mchis zag bzhin du/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di
2b2(mdo): skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das rab tu myur bar mya ngan las 'da' zhing / bde bar gshegs pa rab tu skur bar mya ngan las 'da' ste/ 'jig rten gyi myig rab tu gyun gyi snangal 'gyur/ rab tu myur bar
2b3(mdo): 'jig rten makon ma mchis pa dang / skyabs ma mchis pa dang / yongs su 'dren pa ma mchis par 'gyur ro// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis/ tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo la bka' saHla pa/ kun
2b4(mdo): dga' bo/ chog gis mya ngan ma byed/ smre sngags ma 'don cig/ gang gnas pa dang byung ba dang / 'dus byas dang / bsags pa ni rab tu 'jig pa'i chos can yin pas/ myi 'jig par ga
2b5(mdo): la 'gyur te de ni gnas myed do// kun dga' bo ngas thog ma// nyid du khyed la/ dga' ba dang / sdug pa dang / yid du 'ong ba/ rnams dang / tha dad du 'gyur zhing 'gyes par 'gyur/ bral
2b6(mdo): bar 'gyur bye bar 'gyur ro zhes ma bstand tam/ kun dga' bo khyod kyis pa la byams pa'i lus kyi las phan pa dang / bde ba dang / gnyis su myed pa dang / tshad myed pa dang / myi mthun
2b7(mdo): myed pas bsnyen bkur bar byas so// kun dga' bo kang lha dang / myi dang / lha ma yin gyi 'khor du bcas pa dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas su bcas pa la bskas dpa'am/ bskal pa las lhag par
2b8(mdo): bsnyen bkur byas pa bas/ gang de bzhin gshegs pa la yud tsam cig bsnyed bkur byas pa de/ de bas 'bras bu shi nang tu ches/ kun dga' bo khyod mya ngan byed cig/ smre sngags ma 'don cig/ kun dga' bo khring
2b9(mdo): kyis de bzhin gshegs pa la bsnyen bkur byas pa ni/ don che ba dang / 'bras bu che ba dang / phan yod che ba dang / rgya che ba dang / bdud rtsi dang 'dra ba dang / bdud rtsi'i dnga'abab pa dang / bdud rtsi'i mthar 'gyur ba
3a1(mdo): nas/ mya dpralas 'da' ba'i bar du 'gyur ro// de nas tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bos mchis byis nas/ smre sngags 'dod cing / shibs la zung gi bar du de bzhin gshegs pa seng ge ltar blo g.yas pas mamapa/
3a2(mdo): ba'i gzims mal bcas so// de nas bcom ldan 'das shing sa la bung ga la ba rer gshegs nas/ shing sa la zung ki bar du seng ge ltar glo g.yas pas man la to// gang gi tshe de bzhin gshegs pa shing sa la lung gi
3a3(mdo): bar du med ge ltar klo g.yas pas mnas par gyu ra pa de'i tshe/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams pa/ shing dang rtswa dang / shing shel ba dang / smad dang / rags tshal la sa sor bzhi tsam yan cad ji ma
3a4(mdo): yong pa de dag thams pa dgang dra de bzhis gshegs pa rtsa ma 'ad cher mig pa su gnam/ 'dung / ba tu 'du padu 'dud bar byung // stong gsum kyi stong chen po'i 'dzin da de/
3a5(mdo): khams na/ klung ngas/ 'bab rgyalal/ rba myig gag/ 'us/ steng 'am/ zhon pa'am/ ring ngam/ byad ma dkur po 'bab pa 'i snyed yod pa de dag thams cad sangs rgyas kyi mthus
3a6(mdo): byin gyis brlabs pas kyi 'bab par gyur to// stong gsum kyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi 'ams na/ bya mang po dang / dgas mang po sna tshogs ji snyed yod pa de dag thams cad kyang sangs
3a7(mdo): rgyas kyi mthus smra rdzi 'byin par 'khod cing kyi bgyi rgyu bar gyurang to// stong gsum kyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams na/ nyi ma dang zla ba'i 'od dam/ skam sa'i gzugs sam/ nor bu 'am/ mye 'am/ zin
3a8(mdo): cu rtse cher gyi da 'i snyed yod pa de da thams cad sangs rgyas kyi nas mtshad kyi snang ste/ rlom yin/ smad na ma yid/ skang ngems yin par ma gyur to// stong gsus kyi stong chen po'i 'jig na
3a9(mdo): kyi 'ams na/ sems can dmyal ba chen po'i rtse ci snyed yod pa de dag thams cad kyang sangs rgyas kyi mthus zhi bar gyurang / myi 'bar bar gyur nga / phyim bar gyur da/ myi tshig par gyur / yongs su kyi gdung bar gyur to//
3b1(mdo): stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams na/ kab sems can dmyal ba chen po'i mye de dag thams cad kyang nye bar zhi zhing bsil bar gyur to// de nas sems can dmyas pa'i sems cad de dag thams cad skad
3b2(mdo): cig de dang / yud tsam de'i tshe sangs rgyas kyi mthus bde ba thob par gyur to// dud 'gro'i skye gnas pa'i sems can thams cad kyang / byams pa'i sems dang / phan pa'i sems dang ldan par gyur te/ gcig la
3b3(mdo): gcig gnod sems byed/ rnam par 'tshe ba byed/ nas par 'tho 'tsham pa skyed cing gnod pa byed pa byed par gyur to// gshin rje'i 'jig rten pa'i mamam cad kyang bkres pa dang skom pa myed par gyur to// sems
3b4(mdo): can thams cad kyang skad cig de dang / yud tsam de'ichi/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus bde ba dang / lus dang sems tshim pa dang / sdug bsngal rgyun chad pa dang / bde ba dang / yid bde ba mchog dang ldan
3b5(mdo): bar gyu rang to// de bzhin gshegs pa seng ge ltar glo g.yas pas mnas ma thag tu stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten kyi khams na/ ro'i rgyal po ri rab dang / 'khor yug dang /
3b6(mdo): 'khor yug chen po dang / btang zung dang / btang zung chen po dang / spos kyi ngad sdang dang / gangs ri ci snyed yod pa dang / gzhan yang ri nag po rnams dang / thams cad dang ldan pa'i sa
3b7(mdo): chen po dang / rgya mtsho chen po'i 'khor yug gi 'obs kyi mtha' gtugs pa rnam pa drug tu g.yos te/ 'gul rab tu 'gul/ 'azhugs rab tu 'khrugs/ ldeg rab tu ldeg par gyu rad to// thams cad dang
3b8(mdo): ldan pa'i rlung gi dkyil 'khor yang de'i tshe mye ldang bar gyurar to// de'i tshe skad cig de dang / yud tsam de na sems can thams cad kyang las byed pa rnams btang bar gyur da te/ gnyed myed chod pa myed/ sgrib pa myed
3b9(mdo): rtsom pa myed cing / cang myi zer bar gyur da te/ sgra chung / ca co chung zhing yid myi g.yeng bar gyurd ta/ bcom ldan 'das seng ge ltar klo g.yas pas mnal ma thag tu/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi 'as
4a1(mdo): 'di na lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / myi 'am ni dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten skyong ba

4a6(mdo): non pa brgya phrag bcu la dbang sgyur ba/ 'di snyam du sems shing bdag cag gis sems can 'di dag phrul/ bdag cag gis 'jig rten byas/ bdag cag gis 'jig rten srul to snyam
4a7(mdo): du de ltar shes pa'i tshangs pa dang / tshangs pa chen po stong gsum kyi spyod chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams sa 'khod pa'i dag kyang / rang rang gi stam la mngon par gyi dga' bar gyur to// rang rang gi gnas thams/
4a8(mdo): dang ldan pa yang sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ mogo mog par gyur du par shes so// de bzhin du rangs pa gzhan thams cad kya sangs rgyas kyi mthus rang rang gi gnas rnams sog sog por gyur par shes te/ rang ra/
4a9(mdo): kyi gnas rnams la gyi dka' bar gyu ra to// 'jig rten skyong ba dang / dbang phyug chen po dang / gnas gtsang ma rnams kyang rang rang gi gnas rnams la gyi dgal bar gyur to// de nas stong gsum gyi stong/

5a1(mdo): pa chen po'i zild kyis gnon cing / zil kyis myi non pa/ kun shes pa dang ldan pa brgya phrag bcu la dbang sgyur ba yin te/ bdag gis sems can rnams byas/ bdag gis sems can rnams sru lnga/

6b4(mdo): nam/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das ma lags so// bka' saHla pa/ tshangs pa gang sems can rnams kyi 'bral ba'i sdug bsngal rnam pa sna tshogs pa ma dang / spun dang / sring mo dang /
6b5(mdo): grogs po dang / nye du dang / snag gi gnyen mchis dang / bu pho dang / chung ma dang / bu mo dag dang / bral ba'i sdug bsngal de dag khyod kyis byas shing / khyod kyis su la pa dang / khyod kyis byin
6b6(mdo): kyis brlabs pa yin nam/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das ma lags so// bka' sa lad pa/ gang sems can rnams kyi sdug bsngal sna tshogs ya ba'i las lnga sbyor ba/ skra
6b7(mdo): dang / phabs dang / rgya skyegs dang / 'khor lo 'tshong ba dang / rgya mtsho chen por 'gro ba dang / 'brog dkon par 'jug pa'am/ phyogs sna tshogs su skyabs 'bebs pa'am/ zhing gi las rgya cher byed pa'am/
6b8(mdo): de las gzhan pa'i bya sna tshogs de dag kyang tshangs pa khyod kyis byas shing / khyod kyis stsal pa dang / khyod kyis byin gyis brlabs pa yin nam/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das ma lags so// bka' stsal
6b9(mdo): pa/ tshangs pa gang sems can rnams kyi dge ba dang / myi dge ba'i las rnam pa sna tshogs yang dag par lend pa/ sems cad dmyal ba dang / dud 'gro'i skye gnas dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten dang / lha dang kyi/
7a1(mdo): li rgyu las byung ba rnams dang / gang sems cadan rnams kyi sus dang / ngag dang / yid kyis nyes par gyur pa dang / legs par spyad pa rnams sam/ gang 'jig rten na gyi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam ses/
7a2(mdo): can rnamasas kyi phan pa dang / sdug bsngal ba dang / gnod pa dang / ngan song ngam 'gro log par gyur pa 'di lta ste/ srog gcod pa dang / ma byin par lend pa dang / 'dod pa la log par g.yes pa dang / brdzun/
7a3(mdo): tu smram dang / bra la dang / ngag rtsub mo dang tshig zhus pa dang / banab sems dang / gnod sems dang / log par lta ba de rnams kyang tshangs pa khyod kyis byas shing / thod kyis zhus pa dang / khyod kyis byin gyis
7a4(mdo): brlabs pa yin nas// gso med pa bcom ldan 'das mal gas so// bka' su sa dpa/ tshangs pa gang sems can rnams kyiganod byed kyi sdug bsngal 'di lta ste/ mgo bcad pa 'am/ las
7a5(mdo): rang / rkang pa dang / drwa ba dang sna bcad pa 'am/ sam lag dang / nying lag thams cad bcad pa 'am/ rtser bsregs pa dang / 'dru/ mar gyis gci pa dang / srog dang bral ba dang / ras kyi dang
7a6(mdo): klung dang / mtshon ci gnyis pas btab pa dang / bsad pa dang / bcing ba dang / korang gzhug pa dang / 'jab pa dang / ma / 'gyed ba de dag kya tshangs pa khyod kyis byas shing / thod kyis yus
7a7(mdo): byed kyis brlabs pa sem nas/ gso dang/ com ldan 'das la sa dang semam ca rnams 'dod pa'i myu ngang/ garnas pas sog par stong pangs
7a8(mdo): tham pa ldog par myod pa dang / rgyal dres pa ldan pa sa yog par spyong ba dang / sdig pa'i las thams tsams yin par spyod sde sa parjod kyis kyi zhing / khyod kyis tham dang / khyod kyis kyid
7a9(mdo): brlabs pa yin nam/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das ma lags so// bka' stsal pa/ tshangs pa gang sems can rnams kyi gnod par byed pa/ sna tshogs byad dang / ro langs dang / rigs sngags dang / sngags dang /
7b1(mdo): sman dang / 'byung po dang / gdon 'bebs pa dang / gang de las gzhan pa dug sbyor ba dang / gang sems can rnams la gnod par gyur pa dang / srog dang bral bar 'gyur ba dang / srog 'chad par 'gyur ba de dag kyang tshangs pa/
7b2(mdo): khyod kyis byas shing / khyod kyis sprul pa dang / khyod kyis byin kyis brlabs pa yin nam/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das ma lags so// bka' stsal pa/ gang rigs bzhi 'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du spang
7b3(mdo): du myi rung po'i 'jig rten kyi chos 'di lta ste/ skye ba dang / rga ba dang / na ba dang / 'chi ba dang / s+ya ngan dang / smre sngags 'don pa dang / sdug bsngal ba dang / yid myi bde ba dang / 'azhug pa dang / myi rtag pa'i chos nyid
7b4(mdo): dang / zad pa'i chos nyid dang / 'gyur ba'i chos nyid dang / mdza' ba dang / dka' ba thams cad dang tha dad du 'gyur ba dang / myed par 'gyur/ pra dang / bral bar 'gyur ba dang / bye bar 'gyur pa de dag kyang /
7b5(mdo): tshangs pa khyod kyis byas shing / khyod kyis srul pa dang / khyod/ kyis byin kyis brlabs pa yin nam/ gsol pa/ bcom lda/ na 'das ma lags so// bka' saHlad pa/ tshangs pa ka seMs
7b6(mdo): can rnams kyi 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang / gti mug dang / sgrub pa dang / chod pa dang / bag la nyal ba dang / kun nas bkras pa dang / kun tu sbyor ba rnams dang / de las gzhan pa'i nyon mongs
7b7(mdo): ba 'am pa sna tshogs 'jug pa gang gis/ sems can rnams chags par 'gyur ba dang / sdang bar 'gyur ba dang / rmongs par 'gyur ba dang / las mngon par 'du bya ba rnams pa sna tshogs mngon par 'du byed pa de dag kyang tshangs
7b8(mdo): pa khyod kyis byas shing / khyod kyis sruld pa dang / khyod kyis byin kyis brlabs pa yin nam// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das ma lags so// bka' saHlad pa/ tshangs pa gang 'di sems can dmyas pa dang // dud
7b9(mdo): 'gro'i skye gnas dang / gshin rje la 'jig rten dang / ngan 'gro rnam pa gsum po gang sems can rnams la gnod pa byed pa rnam pa sna tshogs kyis sdug bsngal sna tshogs myong ba de dag kyang tshangs pa khyod kyis byas shing / khyod
8a1(mdo): kyis sus pa dang / khyod kyis byin gyis brlabs pa yin nam/ gsol dab/ bcom ldan 'das ma lags so// bka' ya yad la/ tshangs pa gang 'di 'byung po'i tshogs dang / sa bon gyi tshogs dang /
8a2(mdo): tsa dang / shing shes pa dang / sman dang / nags tshal rgyan gnas pa dang / nga la gnas pa dang / me tog gi zhing dang / 'bras bu log dra dang / spos kyi zhing rnas pa sna tshogs sas/ dang ba dang / ra ba dang / lan dang
8a3(mdo): sgru ba dang / tsA ba dang / bska ba'i mo'i khyad par rnam pa snga tshogs yid du 'ong ba dang / yid du kyi 'ong ba mngon par grub pa/ gang sems can rnams la phan pa dang / gnod par 'gyur ba des ji snyam du sems/ tshangs
8a4(mdo): po de dag khyod kyis byas gang/ khyod kyis yul pa dang / da kyisabyin gyis brlabs pa yin nas/ gsos dang/ bcom ldan 'das su lags so// bka' sa la sa/ sa pa gang 'gro ba lnga /
8a5(mdo): dgas yongs su 'a/ skye ba dang / 'phe 'pho dang / mtshan po dang / 'azus dang / 'dzin pa 'di ga dang / sems cad pa rig pa'i sgrib pa dang / med pa'i dus
8a6(mdo): dang ldan pa/ kun tu rgyug cing 'khor ba de dag gi/ sdod gyi mapa mngon pa dang / tshangs pa ma 'ongs pa'i 'khor ba'i las rgyud ma ra @/ gang na lha dang bcas pa dang / tshangs pa dang bcas pa'i /
8a7(mdo): rten 'di dang / dge sbyong dang / bram ze dang bcas pa'i skye dgu zags 'khrugs pa lta bu/ dru bu 'dzings pa lta bu 'ong ba dang / 'gro bar gyurd pa 'jig rten 'di nas/ 'jig rten pha rol dang / 'jig rten pha rol nas
8a8(mdo): 'jig rten 'dir kun tu rgyug cing 'khor ba/ 'khor ba las 'byung ba gyi shes pa/ de dag la ji snyam du sems/ tshangs pa de dag khyod kyis byas shing / khyod kyis sprul pa dang / khyod kyis byin gyis brlabs pa yin
8a9(mdo): gsol dam/ bcom ldan 'das ma lags so// bad par gshegs pa ma lagasas// bka' sa sa pa yom mam sa kyid tsho'i byi 'di skarangs sems cad 'di dag byas/ ngas rgyal/ gyi
8b1(mdo): kyis brlabs/ ngas 'jig rten byas/ ngas yul/ ngas byin gyis brlabs snyam sems// gsolang pa/ bcom ldan 'das bdag nim 'tshal ba/ rtag tu lta bar gyu rang pa sa spangs pas/ byin dmi log tu
8b2(mdo): gyur pa lags te/ bcom ldan 'das bdag ni de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs pa'i chos 'dul ba rtag tu ma zos pas/ sems can rnams bdag gis bgyis/ bdag gis srul/ 'jig rten bdag gis bgyis/
8b3(mdo): 'jig rten bdag gis 'phruld ces bgyi ba sdig pa can gyi lta bar gyur pa de lta bur gyurd to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa la don 'di nyid bdag zhu'o// bcom ldan 'das 'jig rten 'odi sus bgyis// 'jig
8b4(mdo): rten 'di sus su lang / sems can rnams sus bgyis/ sus yul/ bcom ldan 'das 'di su'i mthu lags/ sus byin kyis brlabs/ de skad ces gsolang pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis tshangs pa
8b5(mdo): de la 'di skad ces bka' sa yang to// tshangs pa 'jig rten no/ las kyis byas/ las kyis su lang to// sems can rnams/ ni las kyis byas/ las kyi rgyu las byung ba/ las kyis
8b6(mdo): rab tu phye'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ tshangs pa ma rig pa'i rkyend kyis 'du byed nams/ 'du byed kyi rkyend kyis rnam par shes pa/ rnam par shes pa'i rkyend kyis myang dang gzugs/ myong dang gzugs
8b7(mdo): kyi rkyen kyis skye mched drug/ skye mched drug gi rkyen kyis reg pa/ reg pa'i rkyedad kyis tshor ba/ tshor ba'i rkyend kyis med pa/ sred pa'i rkyend kyis len pa/ lend pa'i rkyend kyis srid pa/ sred pa'i rkyed kyis
8b8(mdo): skye ba/ skye ba'i rkye nad kyis rgazhi dang / mya ngan dang / smre sngags 'dod pa dang / sdug bsngal ba dang / yid kyi bde ba dang / 'khrug pa rnams byung ste/ de ltar sdug bsngal gyi phung po chen po 'di 'ba' shig byung bar #
8b9(mdo): zhing / tshangs pa ma rig pa/ 'gag pa nas/ sdug bsngal gyi phung po 'ba' shig 'gag pa'i bar su 'gyur te/ tshangs pa yas dang / chos kyi kun tu sbyor ba rnams yod na/ sems can rnams 'byung bar snang ba dang /
9a1(mdo): las dang chos kyi kun tu sbyor ba dang bral bas/ 'byung ba myed par snang ba ma rtogs par 'dis byed pa lo 'amal byed du 'jug pa 'am/ nye bar 'joms pa kapa yang med do// tshangs pa de ltar 'jig rten
9a2(mdo): 'di las zang pa dang / nyon mongs pa khad pa dang / sdug bsngal yang pa dang / sdug bsngal nye bar zhi bas zhi ba dang / nges par 'byung ba dang / rnam pa bzhi pa dang / yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa zhes bya'o// changs
9a3(mdo): bdes/ lam gas yin pa de 'ad pa dang / nyin mongs pagapa smin pa de dang zlas pa dang / sdug bsngal gang yin pa de nas pazhi pa dang / nub pa martogs par yongs su mya nganams 'das pazhes byab me ga yad de//
9a4(mdo): mangs rgyas rnams kyi sa su dang / sangs rgyas rnams kyi kyis kyi thamams kyis chos nyid nga la bu dag zung ngo // dertse'i tsha na/ sangs rgyas com ldan 'das rnams 'byung ba kyangs/
9a5(mdo): lha bu rab tu spyod pa kyi 'byung gi/ tshangs pa gang gi mi sangs/ rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams 'jig rten tu byung ba le'i chen no/ bar bya ba'i phyir 'ong du chud par dka' ba/ zab pa/ zab
9a6(mdo): snang ba/ chos rnas pa de lta bu dag yang dag par ston pa 'gyur te/ de thos pas sems can skye ba'i chos can rnams ni ba las yongs su grol bar 'gyur/ sems cad rga ni dang /
9a7(mdo): dang / smre sngags 'dod pa dang / sdug bsngal ba dang / yid kyi bde ba dang / 'khrug pa'i chos can rnams ni 'jug pa'i babadag las yongs su grol bar 'gyur ro// tshangs pa de lta bas na 'di lta ste/ 'du byed thams cad /
9a8(mdo): myig yor lta bu kyi rtag pa/ g.yo ba/ myi btan pa/ zer zhug ma yin pa/ bad pa dang 'gyur ba'i chos can no zhes/ tshangs pa sangs rgyas rnams kyis de bstan cing yang dag par bshad de/ rnam par phye zhingags pa
9a9(mdo): bar mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas rnams kyi byin kyis rlabs so// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa rnams kyi dam pa'i chos nub pa ma ya pa 'di lta ste/ 'du byed thams cad myig yo lta du'o/
9b1(mdo): zhes bya ba de nyid kyi byed kyi rlabs yin no// gal te de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis 'du byed thams cad kyig sor lta bu mas gzigs su zin na/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams skad cig thang cig yud tsam yang 'du byed
9b2(mdo): thams cad kyi las dang / myig yor dang / zag ma lta bur gyi ston pa zhig na/ tshangs pa gang gi phyir de bzhin gshegs pa rnams 'du byed thams cad skyel ma dang / myig yor dang / zag ma lta bu dang / myi rtag pa dang /
9b3(mdo): g.yo ba dang / 'gyur ba'i chos can du mkhyend pa de'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams 'du byed thams cad kyilas dang / myig yor dang / brag ma lta bur stonang to// de la mkhas pa de'i mtshan ma mthong ba dag yod de/
9b4(mdo): de'i mtsham ma mtho nas/ rgyu de dang / rkyend de dang / dmyigs pa'i mtshan ma nges/ 'du byed thams cad kyi rtag par khong du chud cing / g.yo ba dang / 'gyur ba'i chos can no zhes rnam par 'byed do//
9b5(mdo): 'du byed thams cad ni 'jig cing 'gyur ro// dus dang / tshigs dang / dus tshigs kyis kyang 'jog go// skad cig dang / zang cig/ dang / phyod tsam dang / yud tsam dang / zhag dang / nyi ma dang / !
9b6(mdo): ba dang / zla ba phyed dang / lo dang / lo brgya dang / bskal pa dang / bskal pa brgya dag kyang 'jig par 'gyur ro// mye'i phung po chen po yang 'bar nas shi bar 'gyur ro// chu'i phung po chen po yang bab nas myi
9b7(mdo): 'bab bo// rlung gi phung po chen po a pa langs nas kyi sdang ngo // sa'i phung po chen po yang byung nas myed par 'gyur ro// ri'i phung po chen po 'khor yug dang / 'khor yug chen po dang / lhun po dang / lhun po chen po dang / re/
9b8(mdo): las gzhan pa'i ri nag po dag kyang byung nas myed par 'gyur ro// nyi ma dang / zla ba dang / skar ma'i tshogs kyi 'khor dang bcas pa 'di dag byung nas/ lha mer ma yin/ lhan ner ma yin/ lgang ngem ma yin zhing slar
9b9(mdo): lhung ngo // lha yul pa'i lha'i gzhal myed khang bzang po dag kyang 'jig par 'gyur ro// grong dang / grong khyer dang / grong rdal 'od dag dang / shing ljon pa dang / nags tshal dang / bskyed mos tshal dang / kun dga' ra ba
10a1(mdo): nyams dka' ba 'di dag kyang byung nas 'gag par 'gyur ro// lha dang gyi 'di rnams kyang skye ba dang / rga ba dang / 'pho ba dang / 'byung bar 'gyur ro// skyes bu 'dzangs shing mkhas pa 'di dag kyang mtshan
10a2(mdo): ma de mthong nas/ kye ma'o// 'du byed 'di thams cad ni myi rtag go/ 'dzeg go// 'du byed 'di thams cad myed par 'gro'o// 'gyur ro// 'du byed 'di thams cad bad par 'gyur ro// snyam nas skyo bar 'gyur ro//
10a3(mdo): skyes su 'dzangs shing mkhas pa 'di dag myu de dang / rkyen des khyim nas khyim myed par rab tu 'byung ngo // de dag dad pas khyim nas khyim byed par yang dag par rab tu byung nas kyang / 'du byed thams cad myig so lta bu
10a4(mdo): dang / rgya lam lta bu dang / zag ca lta bur rig ste/ mtshan ma de dang / dmyigs pa de dang / rkye dang nges byang chub thob par 'gyur ro// chu'i nang du zla ba'i dkyis 'khor dang / nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor sdang ba dang / skar sa
10a5(mdo): gzugs sdang ba de dag mthong nas/ de bzhin gshegs pas btams pa'am/ de las gzhan pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis gtams pa'am/ bdag gi blos brtags pas/ 'du byed pa
10a6(mdo): cad kyi lam dang / myig yor dang / zags lta mur rtogs nas dang bas kyis nas kyis myed bur rab tu thung b+he/ chunang tu zhugs pa'abras bu dang / lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang / phyir
10a7(mdo): 'ong ba'i 'bras bu thob pa dang / dgra bcom pa nyid mngon gsum du byed pa dang / gang bag byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa pa bzod pa dang po yob pa dang / bzod pa gnyis pa dang / gsus la thob pa dang / bla na gying
10a8(mdo): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tho par 'gyur ba'i skyes na nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'as kya rangasas 'das pa rnams kyi spos bstad dpa 'di nyi 'jig rted du 'byung ste/ de thos pam mas ca
10a9(mdo): rnams nyan thos kyi theg pa dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa dang / theg pa chen po rga byed gnas se thams cad kyi mchog dang ldan pa dang / theg pa gsum po dag gis nges par 'byung bar 'gyur ro// tshangs pa 'di
10b1(mdo): ska 'dis sangs rgyas rnams kyi byin kyi nubs su rig par bya ste/ ngas pa gang gis skyes bu ma rnas pa dag gis 'du byed 'di dag ni mug bsdul pa/ g.yo ba kyi brtan pa/ zang ba dang / 'thung ba'i chom pa / rtse/
10b2(mdo): las dang / phyig yor dang / zug sa smra bu'o// zhes bya ba'i mtshan ma mthong ras pa drag par spro bar 'gyur ba 'dod/ sangs mnas kyi sras dang / sangs rgyas kyi byed gyi rlabs so// sngon gyur cing sngon gyi
10b3(mdo): 'byung ba'i sems can byed yong+yas su sbya du par byas pa'i dag gis chos kyi sgra 'dis sums ras/ 'du byed 'di dag bams pa na myi rtag pa 'an byed 'asus pa 'dzig pa ste/ 'du bye ma
10b4(mdo): skyel sa dang / zag pa lta bu'i zhes de bzhin gshegs pa la mom par 'gyur/ mngon par dad par 'gyur ro// sems cad gang dag gi sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rlung du ngangs par bya
10b5(mdo): kyang bar 'gyur ba/ kyis par gyur dpas bslab pa'i ga/ zhenams yongs su bzung bar gyur pa de dag kyang / de dang / kye da des 'dis re 'du byed rnams kyi can bu dang / 'du
10b6(mdo): rnams sdug bsngal ba dang / 'du byed rnams 'jig pa dang / 'du byed rnams rgya lam dang / myig yor dang / brag cha lta bu'o zhes 'du byed rnams de lta bu'i tshul du rtogs par 'gyur te/ rgyu de dang /
10b7(mdo): rkyend des dad pas khyim nas khyim myed par rab tu byung nas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams 'jig rten du ma byung yang / sangs rgyas kyi byin kyi rlabs nyid dang / sangs rgyas la dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pal/
10b8(mdo): rkye dad kyis byang chub thob par 'gyur ro// tshangs pa rnam grangs des kyang / 'di ltar 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi byin kyi rlabs dang / 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi yul yin par rig par bya'o// tshangs pa stong gsum gyi stong chen
10b9(mdo): po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'ad yang sangs rgyas kyi/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing yin te/ tshangs pa 'di ni nga sngon byang chub sems dpa'i khyad pa pyod pa na/ bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs myed par/ sangs
11a1(mdo): rgyas bcom ldan 'das cad byed/ grangs myed pa rnams kyi drung du/ dge ba'i rtsa bachad med grangs myed pa bskyed de/ tshul khrims dang / dka' thub dang / tshangs par spyod pa dang / sems gzhan pa'i dka'/
11a2(mdo): bkyang pa bye ba khrag khrig brkyang stong dag gis ji ltar dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad 'phel bar 'gyur ba dang / ji ltar yongs su dag par 'gyur ba dang / dus dang / tshod dang / snod ji lta ba bzhin du 'dul ba nye bar bzung ste/
11a3(mdo): sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su bzung ngo // yongs su sbyangs so// ngas sbyin pa dang / snyan par smra ba dang / don kyang pa dang / don mthun pa bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhi po dag gis sems can rnams yang dag par bsdus te de
11a4(mdo): dag pa'i smon lam nyid kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'dir skyes nasangs chos bstan pa pa yang shes so// pa'i chos bstan bas 'dus pam yang 'gyur te/ brgya byin rnams kyi ma yin/ tshangs pa
11a5(mdo): rnams kyi ma yin/ 'jig rten skyong ba rnams kyi ma yin no// tshangs pa rnams kyis kyang de 'di ltar sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'dzin sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sprin gyi/ brgya byin rnams kyi/
11a6(mdo): ma yin/ tshangs pa rnams kyi ma yin/ 'jig rten skyong ba rnams n+d+hi ma yin/ gzhan mu stegs 'apyod pa can dang / kun tu rgyu ba rnams kyis ma med par rig par bya'o// de nas kyi mched kyi bdag po tshang
11a7(mdo): pa 'bus phrag bcu'i bdag po tshangs pa de dang / de las gzhan pa'i tshangs pa rnams ni skyo zhing / yid byung bar gyur te/ tshig 'di skad ces ci tsam nu sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos rgya chen po dang ldan pa
11a8(mdo): ngo mtshar to// ci tsam du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chad du byung ba'i chos dang ldan pa po mtshar to// zhes smras so// de nas stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i tshangs pa de/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa srang
11a9(mdo): dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la mang du 'dzind par gyur da te/ rtse tsam du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi yul bsam gyis myi khyab cing mtha' yas pa po mtsha rang to snyam mo// de nas stong gsum gyi stong chen
11b1(mdo): po'i tshangs pa chen po de/ bcom ldan 'das kyi slob mar khas blangs nas/ bcom ldan 'das la skyabs su song ste/ bcom ldan 'das ni bdag gi ston pa/ bde bar gshegs pa ni bdag gi ston pa lags na/
11b2(mdo): bcom ldan 'das ji ltar gnas par bgyi ba dang / ji ltar bsgrub par bgyis pa bdag la bka' saHla tu gsol zhes/ bcom ldan 'das la bka' lupa yang nod par gyurd to// de skad ces gsol pa dang

11b4(mdo): kyi'i ngo yin te/ tshangs pa stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di khyongs gtad kyis/ khyod kyis mi nas kyang / pA'i rjes su 'dug par gyis la/ dge ba'i lam 'di dang / dge ba'i tshul 'di dang /

11b6(mdo): zhal nas skyes pa/ chos las byung ba/ chos kyis srul pa/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byams pa snyed rje chen po dang ldan pa/ skye bo mang po'i don 'dod pa/ phan pa 'ad

11b9(mdo): kyi tshul 'di rgyur gyi 'chad par gyis shig/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ tshangs pa ci tsam du dge ba'i tshul 'di lta bu 'di rgyun gyi 'chad par de tsam du/ sangs rgyas kyi tshul dang / chos kyi tshul dang / dge 'dun kyi tshul chur

12a2(mdo): tshangs pa de lta bas na/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'di nyings gtang ngo // tshangs pa khyod la bka' stsas po na 'di yin no// rjes su bsta dad pani 'di yin gyis khyod
